**Step 6.1: Create Login Component**
**File:** `client/src/components/Auth/Login.js`
```javascript
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Form, Input, Button, Card, Row, Col, Tabs, Checkbox, message } from 'antd';
import { MailOutlined, PhoneOutlined, LockOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
import { useAuth } from '../../contexts/AuthContext';
import { useNavigate, Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import UaePassLogin from './UaePassLogin';
import './Auth.css';

const { TabPane } = Tabs;

const Login = () => {
  const [form] = Form.useForm();
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('email');
  const { login } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const handleSubmit = async (values) => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      
      const credentials = {
        password: values.password
      };
      
      if (activeTab === 'email') {
        credentials.email = values.email;
      } else {
        credentials.phone = values.phone;
      }
      
      const result = await login(credentials);
      
      if (result.success) {
        message.success('Login successful!');
        navigate('/dashboard');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Login error:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="auth-container">
      <Row justify="center" align="middle" style={{ minHeight: '100vh' }}>
        <Col xs={24} sm={20} md={16} lg={12} xl={8}>
          <Card className="auth-card">
            <div className="auth-header">
              <h2>Welcome Back</h2>
              <p>Sign in to your White Caves Real Estate account</p>
            </div>
            
            {/* UAE Pass Login Section */}
            <div className="uaepass-section">
              <UaePassLogin />
              <div className="divider">
                <span>or continue with</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            {/* Email/Phone Login Tabs */}
            <Tabs activeKey={activeTab} onChange={setActiveTab} className="auth-tabs">
              <TabPane tab={<span><MailOutlined /> Email</span>} key="email">
                <Form
                  form={form}
                  name="email-login"
                  onFinish={handleSubmit}
                  layout="vertical"
                  initialValues={{ remember: true }}
                >
                  <Form.Item
                    name="email"
                    label="Email Address"
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please enter your email!' },
                      { type: 'email', message: 'Please enter a valid email!' }
                    ]}
                  >
                    <Input
                      prefix={<MailOutlined />}
                      placeholder="Enter your email"
                      size="large"
                    />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="password"
                    label="Password"
                    rules={[{ required: true, message: 'Please enter your password!' }]}
                  >
                    <Input.Password
                      prefix={<LockOutlined />}
                      placeholder="Enter your password"
                      size="large"
                    />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item>
                    <div className="form-options">
                      <Form.Item name="remember" valuePropName="checked" noStyle>
                        <Checkbox>Remember me</Checkbox>
                      </Form.Item>
                      <Link to="/forgot-password">Forgot password?</Link>
                    </div>
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item>
                    <Button
                      type="primary"
                      htmlType="submit"
                      size="large"
                      loading={loading}
                      block
                    >
                      Sign In with Email
                    </Button>
                  </Form.Item>
                </Form>
              </TabPane>
              
              <TabPane tab={<span><PhoneOutlined /> Phone</span>} key="phone">
                <Form
                  form={form}
                  name="phone-login"
                  onFinish={handleSubmit}
                  layout="vertical"
                  initialValues={{ remember: true }}
                >
                  <Form.Item
                    name="phone"
                    label="Phone Number"
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please enter your phone number!' },
                      { pattern: /^(\+971|00971|0)?(5[0-9]{8})$/, message: 'Please enter a valid UAE phone number' }
                    ]}
                  >
                    <Input
                      prefix={<PhoneOutlined />}
                      placeholder="+971 50 123 4567"
                      size="large"
                    />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="password"
                    label="Password"
                    rules={[{ required: true, message: 'Please enter your password!' }]}
                  >
                    <Input.Password
                      prefix={<LockOutlined />}
                      placeholder="Enter your password"
                      size="large"
                    />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item>
                    <div className="form-options">
                      <Form.Item name="remember" valuePropName="checked" noStyle>
                        <Checkbox>Remember me</Checkbox>
                      </Form.Item>
                      <Link to="/forgot-password?method=phone">Forgot password?</Link>
                    </div>
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item>
                    <Button
                      type="primary"
                      htmlType="submit"
                      size="large"
                      loading={loading}
                      block
                    >
                      Sign In with Phone
                    </Button>
                  </Form.Item>
                </Form>
              </TabPane>
            </Tabs>
            
            <div className="auth-footer">
              <p>
                Don't have an account?{' '}
                <Link to="/register">Sign up here</Link>
              </p>
            </div>
          </Card>
        </Col>
      </Row>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Login;
```

**Step 6.2: Create UAE Pass Login Component**
**File:** `client/src/components/Auth/UaePassLogin.js`
```javascript
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Button, Modal, Steps, Alert } from 'antd';
import { IdcardOutlined, MobileOutlined, DesktopOutlined, CheckCircleOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
import axios from 'axios';
import './Auth.css';

const { Step } = Steps;

const UaePassLogin = () => {
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [showMobileOptions, setShowMobileOptions] = useState(false);
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(0);

  const initiateUaePassLogin = async (isMobile = false) => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      setCurrentStep(1);
      
      const response = await axios.get('/api/uaepass/initiate');
      
      if (response.data.success) {
        if (isMobile && response.data.isMobile) {
          // Try to open UAE Pass app via deep link
          window.location.href = `uaepass://authorize?state=${response.data.state}&nonce=${response.data.nonce}`;
          
          // Fallback to web after delay
          setTimeout(() => {
            window.location.href = response.data.authUrl;
          }, 2000);
        } else {
          // Direct web flow
          window.location.href = response.data.authUrl;
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Failed to initiate UAE Pass:', error);
      setLoading(false);
      setCurrentStep(0);
    }
  };

  const handleWebLogin = () => {
    initiateUaePassLogin(false);
  };

  const handleMobileAppLogin = () => {
    initiateUaePassLogin(true);
  };

  return (
    <div className="uaepass-login-container">
      <Steps current={currentStep} size="small" className="uaepass-steps">
        <Step title="Choose Method" />
        <Step title="Authenticate" />
        <Step title="Verified" />
      </Steps>
      
      {currentStep === 0 && (
        <div className="login-methods">
          <Button
            type="primary"
            size="large"
            icon={<IdcardOutlined />}
            onClick={() => setShowMobileOptions(true)}
            block
            style={{ marginBottom: '16px' }}
          >
            Login with UAE Pass
          </Button>
          
          <Modal
            title="Choose UAE Pass Login Method"
            visible={showMobileOptions}
            onCancel={() => setShowMobileOptions(false)}
            footer={null}
            centered
          >
            <div className="mobile-options">
              <Button
                type="primary"
                size="large"
                icon={<MobileOutlined />}
                onClick={handleMobileAppLogin}
                block
                style={{ marginBottom: '12px' }}
                loading={loading}
              >
                Open UAE Pass App
              </Button>
              
              <Button
                type="default"
                size="large"
                icon={<DesktopOutlined />}
                onClick={handleWebLogin}
                block
                loading={loading}
              >
                Use Web Browser
              </Button>
            </div>
          </Modal>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {currentStep === 1 && (
        <div className="authenticating">
          <Alert
            message="Redirecting to UAE Pass"
            description="Please complete the verification in the UAE Pass app or website."
            type="info"
            showIcon
          />
        </div>
      )}
      
      <div className="uaepass-benefits">
        <h4>Benefits of UAE Pass:</h4>
        <ul>
          <li><CheckCircleOutlined /> Government-verified identity</li>
          <li><CheckCircleOutlined /> No passwords needed</li>
          <li><CheckCircleOutlined /> Secure and encrypted</li>
          <li><CheckCircleOutlined /> Fast and convenient</li>
        </ul>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default UaePassLogin;
```

**Step 6.3: Create Registration Component**
**File:** `client/src/components/Auth/Register.js`
```javascript
import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { Form, Input, Button, Card, Row, Col, Steps, Select, message } from 'antd';
import { useAuth } from '../../contexts/AuthContext';
import { useNavigate, Link } from 'react-router-dom';
import './Auth.css';

const { Step } = Steps;
const { Option } = Select;

const Register = () => {
  const [form] = Form.useForm();
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [currentStep, setCurrentStep] = useState(0);
  const { register } = useAuth();
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const steps = [
    {
      title: 'Account Type',
      content: 'Choose your account type'
    },
    {
      title: 'Personal Info',
      content: 'Enter your personal information'
    },
    {
      title: 'Verification',
      content: 'Verify your account'
    }
  ];

  const handleSubmit = async (values) => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      
      const userData = {
        email: values.email,
        phone: values.phone,
        password: values.password,
        firstName: values.firstName,
        lastName: values.lastName,
        role: values.accountType
      };
      
      const result = await register(userData);
      
      if (result.success) {
        if (result.data.requiresVerification) {
          setCurrentStep(2);
          message.success('Registration successful! Please check your email for verification.');
        } else {
          message.success('Registration successful!');
          navigate('/dashboard');
        }
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Registration error:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="auth-container">
      <Row justify="center" align="middle" style={{ minHeight: '100vh' }}>
        <Col xs={24} sm={20} md={16} lg={12} xl={8}>
          <Card className="auth-card">
            <div className="auth-header">
              <h2>Create Account</h2>
              <p>Join White Caves Real Estate platform</p>
            </div>
            
            <Steps current={currentStep} className="registration-steps">
              {steps.map((step, index) => (
                <Step key={index} title={step.title} />
              ))}
            </Steps>
            
            <Form
              form={form}
              name="register"
              onFinish={handleSubmit}
              layout="vertical"
              scrollToFirstError
            >
              {currentStep === 0 && (
                <div className="step-content">
                  <Form.Item
                    name="accountType"
                    label="Account Type"
                    rules={[{ required: true, message: 'Please select account type!' }]}
                  >
                    <Select placeholder="Select account type" size="large">
                      <Option value="client">Client / Buyer</Option>
                      <Option value="tenant">Tenant / Renter</Option>
                      <Option value="agent">Real Estate Agent</Option>
                      <Option value="owner">Property Owner</Option>
                    </Select>
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <div className="step-actions">
                    <Button
                      type="primary"
                      onClick={() => setCurrentStep(1)}
                      size="large"
                      block
                    >
                      Next
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
              
              {currentStep === 1 && (
                <div className="step-content">
                  <Form.Item
                    name="email"
                    label="Email Address"
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please enter your email!' },
                      { type: 'email', message: 'Please enter a valid email!' }
                    ]}
                  >
                    <Input placeholder="Enter your email" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="phone"
                    label="Phone Number"
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please enter your phone number!' },
                      { pattern: /^(\+971|00971|0)?(5[0-9]{8})$/, message: 'Please enter a valid UAE phone number' }
                    ]}
                  >
                    <Input placeholder="+971 50 123 4567" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="password"
                    label="Password"
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please enter your password!' },
                      { min: 8, message: 'Password must be at least 8 characters!' }
                    ]}
                    hasFeedback
                  >
                    <Input.Password placeholder="Enter your password" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="confirmPassword"
                    label="Confirm Password"
                    dependencies={['password']}
                    hasFeedback
                    rules={[
                      { required: true, message: 'Please confirm your password!' },
                      ({ getFieldValue }) => ({
                        validator(_, value) {
                          if (!value || getFieldValue('password') === value) {
                            return Promise.resolve();
                          }
                          return Promise.reject(new Error('Passwords do not match!'));
                        },
                      }),
                    ]}
                  >
                    <Input.Password placeholder="Confirm your password" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="firstName"
                    label="First Name"
                    rules={[{ required: true, message: 'Please enter your first name!' }]}
                  >
                    <Input placeholder="Enter your first name" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <Form.Item
                    name="lastName"
                    label="Last Name"
                    rules={[{ required: true, message: 'Please enter your last name!' }]}
                  >
                    <Input placeholder="Enter your last name" size="large" />
                  </Form.Item>
                  
                  <div className="step-actions">
                    <Button
                      type="default"
                      onClick={() => setCurrentStep(0)}
                      size="large"
                      style={{ marginRight: 8 }}
                    >
                      Back
                    </Button>
                    <Button
                      type="primary"
                      htmlType="submit"
                      size="large"
                      loading={loading}
                    >
                      Register
                    </Button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
              
              {currentStep === 2 && (
                <div className="step-content">
                  <div className="verification-message">
                    <h3>Check Your Email</h3>
                    <p>We've sent a verification link to your email address.</p>
                    <p>Please click the link in the email to verify your account.</p>
                    
                    <div className="verification-actions">
                      <Button type="primary" onClick={() => navigate('/login')}>
                        Go to Login
                      </Button>
                      <Button type="link" onClick={() => message.info('Resend email functionality coming soon')}>
                        Resend Verification Email
                      </Button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </Form>
            
            <div className="auth-footer">
              <p>
                Already have an account?{' '}
                <Link to="/login">Sign in here</Link>
              </p>
            </div>
          </Card>
        </Col>
      </Row>
    </div>
  );
};

export default Register;
```

### **PHASE 7: PROPERTY MANAGEMENT MODULE (Day 4-5)**
**Estimated Time:** 6-8 hours

**Step 7.1: Create Property List Component**
**File:** `client/src/components/Properties/PropertyList.js`
```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Row, Col, Card, Input, Select, Button, Pagination, Spin, Empty } from 'antd';
import { SearchOutlined, FilterOutlined } from '@ant-design/icons';
import PropertyCard from './PropertyCard';
import axios from 'axios';
import './PropertyList.css';

const { Search } = Input;
const { Option } = Select;

const PropertyList = () => {
  const [properties, setProperties] = useState([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [filters, setFilters] = useState({
    emirate: '',
    propertyType: '',
    minPrice: '',
    maxPrice: '',
    bedrooms: '',
    search: ''
  });
  const [pagination, setPagination] = useState({
    current: 1,
    pageSize: 12,
    total: 0
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchProperties();
  }, [filters, pagination.current]);

  const fetchProperties = async () => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      
      const params = {
        page: pagination.current,
        limit: pagination.pageSize,
        ...filters
      };
      
      const response = await axios.get('/api/properties', { params });
      
      setProperties(response.data.properties || []);
      setPagination(prev => ({
        ...prev,
        total: response.data.total || 0
      }));
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching properties:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const handleSearch = (value) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, search: value }));
    setPagination(prev => ({ ...prev, current: 1 }));
  };

  const handleFilterChange = (key, value) => {
    setFilters(prev => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }));
    setPagination(prev => ({ ...prev, current: 1 }));
  };

  const handlePageChange = (page) => {
    setPagination(prev => ({ ...prev, current: page }));
  };

  const clearFilters = () => {
    setFilters({
      emirate: '',
      propertyType: '',
      minPrice: '',
      maxPrice: '',
      bedrooms: '',
      search: ''
    });
    setPagination(prev => ({ ...prev, current: 1 }));
  };

  if (loading && properties.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="loading-container">
        <Spin size="large" />
        <p>Loading properties...</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="property-list-container">
      {/* Search and Filter Section */}
      <Card className="filters-card">
        <Row gutter={[16, 16]} align="middle">
          <Col xs={24} md={8}>
            <Search
              placeholder="Search properties..."
              allowClear
              enterButton={<SearchOutlined />}
              size="large"
              onSearch={handleSearch}
              onChange={(e) => handleFilterChange('search', e.target.value)}
              value={filters.search}
            />
          </Col>
          
          <Col xs={24} md={16}>
            <Row gutter={[8, 8]}>
              <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
                <Select
                  placeholder="Emirate"
                  size="large"
                  style={{ width: '100%' }}
                  value={filters.emirate || undefined}
                  onChange={(value) => handleFilterChange('emirate', value)}
                  allowClear
                >
                  <Option value="Dubai">Dubai</Option>
                  <Option value="Abu Dhabi">Abu Dhabi</Option>
                  <Option value="Sharjah">Sharjah</Option>
                  <Option value="Ajman">Ajman</Option>
                  <Option value="Ras Al Khaimah">Ras Al Khaimah</Option>
                  <Option value="Fujairah">Fujairah</Option>
                  <Option value="Umm Al Quwain">Umm Al Quwain</Option>
                </Select>
              </Col>
              
              <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
                <Select
                  placeholder="Type"
                  size="large"
                  style={{ width: '100%' }}
                  value={filters.propertyType || undefined}
                  onChange={(value) => handleFilterChange('propertyType', value)}
                  allowClear
                >
                  <Option value="Apartment">Apartment</Option>
                  <Option value="Villa">Villa</Option>
                  <Option value="Townhouse">Townhouse</Option>
                  <Option value="Penthouse">Penthouse</Option>
                  <Option value="Office">Office</Option>
                  <Option value="Warehouse">Warehouse</Option>
                  <Option value="Land">Land</Option>
                  <Option value="Commercial">Commercial</Option>
                </Select>
              </Col>
              
              <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
                <Select
                  placeholder="Bedrooms"
                  size="large"
                  style={{ width: '100%' }}
                  value={filters.bedrooms || undefined}
                  onChange={(value) => handleFilterChange('bedrooms', value)}
                  allowClear
                >
                  <Option value="1">1 Bedroom</Option>
                  <Option value="2">2 Bedrooms</Option>
                  <Option value="3">3 Bedrooms</Option>
                  <Option value="4">4 Bedrooms</Option>
                  <Option value="5">5+ Bedrooms</Option>
                </Select>
              </Col>
              
              <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
                <Button
                  type="default"
                  icon={<FilterOutlined />}
                  size="large"
                  onClick={clearFilters}
                  style={{ width: '100%' }}
                >
                  Clear Filters
                </Button>
              </Col>
            </Row>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>
      
      {/* Property Grid */}
      {properties.length === 0 ? (
        <Empty
          description="No properties found"
          image={Empty.PRESENTED_IMAGE_SIMPLE}
          style={{ margin: '50px 0' }}
        />
      ) : (
        <>
          <Row gutter={[24, 24]} className="property-grid">
            {properties.map(property => (
              <Col key={property._id} xs={24} sm={12} lg={8} xl={6}>
                <PropertyCard property={property} />
              </Col>
            ))}
          </Row>
          
          {/* Pagination */}
          {pagination.total > pagination.pageSize && (
            <div className="pagination-container">
              <Pagination
                current={pagination.current}
                pageSize={pagination.pageSize}
                total={pagination.total}
                onChange={handlePageChange}
                showSizeChanger={false}
                showQuickJumper
              />
            </div>
          )}
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default PropertyList;
```

**Step 7.2: Create Property Card Component**
**File:** `client/src/components/Properties/PropertyCard.js`
```javascript
import React from 'react';
import { Card, Tag, Button, Row, Col } from 'antd';
import { 
  BedOutlined, 
  BathOutlined, 
  AreaChartOutlined, 
  LocationOutlined,
  EyeOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import './PropertyCard.css';

const { Meta } = Card;

const PropertyCard = ({ property }) => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const getStatusColor = (status) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'available': return 'green';
      case 'reserved': return 'orange';
      case 'under_contract': return 'blue';
      case 'sold': return 'red';
      case 'rented': return 'purple';
      default: return 'default';
    }
  };

  const getStatusText = (status) => {
    switch (status) {
      case 'available': return 'Available';
      case 'reserved': return 'Reserved';
      case 'under_contract': return 'Under Contract';
      case 'sold': return 'Sold';
      case 'rented': return 'Rented';
      default: return status;
    }
  };

  const handleViewDetails = () => {
    navigate(`/properties/${property._id}`);
  };

  const primaryImage = property.images?.find(img => img.isPrimary) || property.images?.[0];

  return (
    <Card
      hoverable
      className="property-card"
      cover={
        <div className="property-image-container">
          {primaryImage ? (
            <img
              alt={property.propertyCode}
              src={primaryImage.url}
              className="property-image"
            />
          ) : (
            <div className="property-image-placeholder">
              <AreaChartOutlined style={{ fontSize: '48px', color: '#ccc' }} />
            </div>
          )}
          <Tag 
            color={getStatusColor(property.status.current)} 
            className="property-status-tag"
          >
            {getStatusText(property.status.current)}
          </Tag>
          {property.views > 0 && (
            <div className="property-views">
              <EyeOutlined /> {property.views}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      }
      actions={[
        <Button type="primary" onClick={handleViewDetails}>
          View Details
        </Button>
      ]}
    >
      <Meta
        title={
          <div className="property-title">
            <h3>{property.propertyCode}</h3>
            <div className="property-price">
              {property.pricing.amount.toLocaleString()} {property.pricing.currency}
              <span className="property-type">
                / {property.pricing.type === 'sale' ? 'Sale' : 'Rent'}
              </span>
            </div>
          </div>
        }
        description={
          <>
            <div className="property-location">
              <LocationOutlined /> {property.emirate}, {property.community}
            </div>
            
            <Row gutter={[8, 8]} className="property-features">
              <Col span={8}>
                <div className="feature-item">
                  <BedOutlined />
                  <span>{property.specifications.bedrooms || 0} Beds</span>
                </div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={8}>
                <div className="feature-item">
                  <BathOutlined />
                  <span>{property.specifications.bathrooms || 0} Baths</span>
                </div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={8}>
                <div className="feature-item">
                  <AreaChartOutlined />
                  <span>{property.specifications.builtUpArea || 0} sqft</span>
                </div>
              </Col>
            </Row>
            
            <div className="property-description">
              {property.specifications.propertyType} â€¢ {property.specifications.yearBuilt || 'N/A'}
            </div>
          </>
        }
      />
    </Card>
  );
};

export default PropertyCard;
```

**Step 8.2: Create Main Dashboard**
**File:** `client/src/components/Dashboard/MainDashboard.js`
```javascript
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Row, Col, Card, Statistic, Table, Button, Select, DatePicker } from 'antd';
import { 
  PropertySafetyOutlined,
  TeamOutlined,
  DollarOutlined,
  MessageOutlined,
  ArrowUpOutlined,
  ArrowDownOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';
import DashboardLayout from './DashboardLayout';
import axios from 'axios';
import './Dashboard.css';

const { RangePicker } = DatePicker;
const { Option } = Select;

const MainDashboard = () => {
  const [dashboardData, setDashboardData] = useState({
    summary: {},
    recentProperties: [],
    topAgents: [],
    recentLeads: []
  });
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [dateRange, setDateRange] = useState([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchDashboardData();
  }, [dateRange]);

  const fetchDashboardData = async () => {
    try {
      setLoading(true);
      
      const params = {};
      if (dateRange.length === 2) {
        params.startDate = dateRange[0].format('YYYY-MM-DD');
        params.endDate = dateRange[1].format('YYYY-MM-DD');
      }
      
      const response = await axios.get('/api/dashboard/summary', { params });
      setDashboardData(response.data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error fetching dashboard data:', error);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const statCards = [
    {
      title: 'Total Properties',
      value: dashboardData.summary?.totalProperties || 0,
      icon: <PropertySafetyOutlined />,
      color: '#1890ff',
      change: '+12%',
      trend: 'up'
    },
    {
      title: 'Active Agents',
      value: dashboardData.summary?.activeAgents || 0,
      icon: <TeamOutlined />,
      color: '#52c41a',
      change: '+5%',
      trend: 'up'
    },
    {
      title: 'Monthly Revenue',
      value: `AED ${(dashboardData.summary?.monthlyRevenue || 0).toLocaleString()}`,
      icon: <DollarOutlined />,
      color: '#faad14',
      change: '+18%',
      trend: 'up'
    },
    {
      title: 'New Leads',
      value: dashboardData.summary?.newLeads || 0,
      icon: <MessageOutlined />,
      color: '#722ed1',
      change: '+25%',
      trend: 'up'
    }
  ];

  const propertyColumns = [
    {
      title: 'Property Code',
      dataIndex: 'propertyCode',
      key: 'propertyCode'
    },
    {
      title: 'Type',
      dataIndex: ['specifications', 'propertyType'],
      key: 'type'
    },
    {
      title: 'Location',
      dataIndex: 'emirate',
      key: 'location'
    },
    {
      title: 'Price',
      dataIndex: ['pricing', 'amount'],
      key: 'price',
      render: (price) => `AED ${price.toLocaleString()}`
    },
    {
      title: 'Status',
      dataIndex: ['status', 'current'],
      key: 'status',
      render: (status) => (
        <span className={`status-badge status-${status}`}>
          {status.replace('_', ' ').toUpperCase()}
        </span>
      )
    }
  ];

  const agentColumns = [
    {
      title: 'Agent',
      dataIndex: 'name',
      key: 'name'
    },
    {
      title: 'Properties',
      dataIndex: 'propertiesCount',
      key: 'propertiesCount'
    },
    {
      title: 'Leads',
      dataIndex: 'leadsCount',
      key: 'leadsCount'
    },
    {
      title: 'Conversion',
      dataIndex: 'conversionRate',
      key: 'conversionRate',
      render: (rate) => `${rate}%`
    },
    {
      title: 'Rating',
      dataIndex: 'rating',
      key: 'rating',
      render: (rating) => `${rating}/5`
    }
  ];

  return (
    <DashboardLayout>
      <div className="dashboard-container">
        <div className="dashboard-header">
          <h1>Dashboard Overview</h1>
          <div className="dashboard-controls">
            <RangePicker 
              onChange={setDateRange}
              style={{ marginRight: 16 }}
            />
            <Button type="primary" onClick={fetchDashboardData}>
              Refresh
            </Button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Stats Cards */}
        <Row gutter={[16, 16]} className="stats-row">
          {statCards.map((stat, index) => (
            <Col xs={24} sm={12} lg={6} key={index}>
              <Card>
                <Statistic
                  title={stat.title}
                  value={stat.value}
                  prefix={stat.icon}
                  valueStyle={{ color: stat.color }}
                />
                <div className="stat-change">
                  <span className={`trend-${stat.trend}`}>
                    {stat.trend === 'up' ? <ArrowUpOutlined /> : <ArrowDownOutlined />}
                    {stat.change}
                  </span>
                  <span> from last month</span>
                </div>
              </Card>
            </Col>
          ))}
        </Row>
        
        {/* Charts and Tables */}
        <Row gutter={[16, 16]} className="charts-row">
          <Col xs={24} lg={12}>
            <Card title="Recent Properties" className="dashboard-card">
              <Table
                columns={propertyColumns}
                dataSource={dashboardData.recentProperties}
                pagination={{ pageSize: 5 }}
                rowKey="_id"
                loading={loading}
              />
            </Card>
          </Col>
          
          <Col xs={24} lg={12}>
            <Card title="Top Performing Agents" className="dashboard-card">
              <Table
                columns={agentColumns}
                dataSource={dashboardData.topAgents}
                pagination={{ pageSize: 5 }}
                rowKey="_id"
                loading={loading}
              />
            </Card>
          </Col>
        </Row>
        
        {/* Quick Actions */}
        <Card title="Quick Actions" className="quick-actions-card">
          <Row gutter={[16, 16]}>
            <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
              <Button type="primary" block onClick={() => window.location.href = '/dashboard/properties/add'}>
                Add Property
              </Button>
            </Col>
            <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
              <Button type="default" block onClick={() => window.location.href = '/dashboard/agents/add'}>
                Add Agent
              </Button>
            </Col>
            <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
              <Button type="default" block onClick={() => window.location.href = '/dashboard/reports'}>
                Generate Report
              </Button>
            </Col>
            <Col xs={12} sm={6}>
              <Button type="default" block onClick={() => window.location.href = '/dashboard/settings'}>
                Settings
              </Button>
            </Col>
          </Row>
        </Card>
      </div>
    </DashboardLayout>
  );
};

export default MainDashboard;
```

**Step 9.3: Write Unit Tests**
**File:** `client/src/__tests__/AuthContext.test.js`
```javascript
import React from 'react';
import { render, waitFor, act } from '@testing-library/react';
import { AuthProvider, useAuth } from '../contexts/AuthContext';
import axios from 'axios';

// Mock axios
jest.mock('axios');

const TestComponent = () => {
  const { user, isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  return (
    <div>
      <span data-testid="user">{JSON.stringify(user)}</span>
      <span data-testid="authenticated">{isAuthenticated.toString()}</span>
    </div>
  );
};

describe('AuthContext', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    localStorage.clear();
    jest.clearAllMocks();
  });

  test('should load user when token exists', async () => {
    const mockUser = { id: '1', email: 'test@example.com' };
    axios.get.mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: mockUser } });
    
    localStorage.setItem('token', 'test-token');
    
    await act(async () => {
      render(
        <AuthProvider>
          <TestComponent />
        </AuthProvider>
      );
    });
    
    await waitFor(() => {
      expect(axios.get).toHaveBeenCalledWith('/api/auth/profile');
    });
  });

  test('should handle login error', async () => {
    axios.post.mockRejectedValue(new Error('Login failed'));
    
    const { result } = renderHook(() => useAuth(), {
      wrapper: AuthProvider
    });
    
    await act(async () => {
      const loginResult = await result.current.login({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'password'
      });
      
      expect(loginResult.success).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});
```

**Step 9.4: Write Server Tests**
**File:** `server/tests/auth.test.js`
```javascript
const request = require('supertest');
const app = require('../server');
const User = require('../models/User');
const mongoose = require('mongoose');

describe('Authentication API', () => {
  beforeAll(async () => {
    await mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI_TEST, {
      useNewUrlParser: true,
      useUnifiedTopology: true,
    });
  });

  afterAll(async () => {
    await mongoose.connection.close();
  });

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await User.deleteMany({});
  });

  describe('POST /api/auth/register', () => {
    it('should register a new user', async () => {
      const userData = {
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'Password123',
        firstName: 'John',
        lastName: 'Doe',
        phone: '+971501234567'
      };

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/register')
        .send(userData)
        .expect(201);

      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('success', true);
      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('token');
      expect(response.body.user).toHaveProperty('email', 'test@example.com');
    });

    it('should reject duplicate email registration', async () => {
      await User.create({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'Password123',
        profile: { firstName: 'John', lastName: 'Doe' }
      });

      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/register')
        .send({
          email: 'test@example.com',
          password: 'Password123',
          firstName: 'Jane',
          lastName: 'Doe'
        })
        .expect(400);

      expect(response.body.success).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('POST /api/auth/login', () => {
    beforeEach(async () => {
      await User.create({
        email: 'test@example.com',
        password: 'Password123',
        profile: { firstName: 'John', lastName: 'Doe' },
        status: 'active'
      });
    });

    it('should login with valid credentials', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@example.com',
          password: 'Password123'
        })
        .expect(200);

      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('success', true);
      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('token');
      expect(response.body.user.email).toBe('test@example.com');
    });

    it('should reject invalid credentials', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@example.com',
          password: 'WrongPassword'
        })
        .expect(401);

      expect(response.body.success).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});
```

**Step 10.2: Create Docker Configuration**
**File:** `Dockerfile`
```dockerfile
# Build stage
FROM node:18-alpine as build

WORKDIR /app

# Copy package files
COPY package*.json ./
COPY client/package*.json ./client/
COPY server/package*.json ./server/

# Install dependencies
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Build client
WORKDIR /app/client
RUN npm run build

# Production stage
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Copy built files
COPY --from=build /app/package*.json ./
COPY --from=build /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=build /app/server ./server
COPY --from=build /app/client/build ./client/build

# Set environment variables
ENV NODE_ENV=production
ENV PORT=3000

EXPOSE 3000

CMD ["node", "server/server.js"]
```

**File:** `docker-compose.yml`

version: '3.8'

services:
  mongodb:
    image: mongo:6
    container_name: whitecaves-mongodb
    restart: unless-stopped
    environment:
      MONGO_INITDB_ROOT_USERNAME: admin
      MONGO_INITDB_ROOT_PASSWORD: ${MONGODB_PASSWORD}
      MONGO_INITDB_DATABASE: whitecaves
    volumes:
      - mongodb_data:/data/db
    ports:
      - "27017:27017"
    networks:
      - whitecaves-network

  app:
    build: .
    container_name: whitecaves-app
    restart: unless-stopped
    depends_on:
      - mongodb
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      MONGODB_URI: mongodb://admin:${MONGODB_PASSWORD}@mongodb:27017/whitecaves?authSource=admin
      JWT_SECRET: ${JWT_SECRET}
      PORT: 3000
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    networks:
      - whitecaves-network
    volumes:
      - ./uploads:/app/uploads

  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    container_name: whitecaves-nginx
    restart: unless-stopped
    depends_on:
      - app
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      - "443:443"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf
      - ./ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl
    networks:
      - whitecaves-network

volumes:
  mongodb_data:

networks:
  whitecaves-network:

**Step 10.3: Create NGINX Configuration**
**File:** `nginx.conf`
```nginx
events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    upstream nodejs_backend {
        server app:3000;
    }

    server {
        listen 80;
        server_name whitecaves.com www.whitecaves.com;
        
        # Redirect to HTTPS
        return 301 https://$server_name$request_uri;
    }

    server {
        listen 443 ssl http2;
        server_name whitecaves.com www.whitecaves.com;

        ssl_certificate /etc/nginx/ssl/whitecaves.crt;
        ssl_certificate_key /etc/nginx/ssl/whitecaves.key;
        
        ssl_protocols TLSv1.2 TLSv1.3;
        ssl_ciphers HIGH:!aNULL:!MD5;

        # Security headers
        add_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;
        add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;
        add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;

        # Static files
        location /static/ {
            alias /app/client/build/static/;
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, immutable";
        }

        # API requests
        location /api/ {
            proxy_pass http://nodejs_backend;
            proxy_http_version 1.1;
            proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
            proxy_set_header Connection 'upgrade';
            proxy_set_header Host $host;
            proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
            proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
            proxy_cache_bypass $http_upgrade;
        }

        # Frontend
        location / {
            root /app/client/build;
            try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
            expires 1h;
            add_header Cache-Control "public";
        }

        # Gzip compression
        gzip on;
        gzip_vary on;
        gzip_min_length 1024;
        gzip_types
            text/plain
            text/css
            text/xml
            text/javascript
            application/json
            application/javascript
            application/xml+rss
            application/atom+xml
            image/svg+xml;
    }
}
```

### **PHASE 11: MONITORING & MAINTENANCE (Ongoing)**
**Estimated Time:** Ongoing

**Step 11.1: Create Monitoring Dashboard**
**File:** `server/monitoring/health.js`
```javascript
const os = require('os');
const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const healthCheck = async () => {
  const health = {
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    uptime: process.uptime(),
    system: {
      memory: {
        total: os.totalmem(),
        free: os.freemem(),
        used: os.totalmem() - os.freemem()
      },
      cpu: os.cpus(),
      load: os.loadavg()
    },
    database: {
      status: 'unknown',
      latency: 0
    },
    services: {}
  };

  try {
    // Check database connection
    const dbStart = Date.now();
    await mongoose.connection.db.admin().ping();
    const dbLatency = Date.now() - dbStart;
    
    health.database = {
      status: 'connected',
      latency: dbLatency,
      collections: await mongoose.connection.db.listCollections().toArray()
    };
  } catch (error) {
    health.database = {
      status: 'disconnected',
      error: error.message
    };
    health.status = 'unhealthy';
  }

  return health;
};

module.exports = { healthCheck };
```

**Step 11.2: Create Logging Configuration**
**File:** `server/utils/logger.js`
```javascript
const winston = require('winston');
const path = require('path');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? 'info' : 'debug',
  format: winston.format.combine(
    winston.format.timestamp(),
    winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
    winston.format.json()
  ),
  transports: [
    // Write all logs with importance level of `error` or less to `error.log`
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(__dirname, '../logs/error.log'), 
      level: 'error' 
    }),
    
    // Write all logs with importance level of `info` or less to `combined.log`
    new winston.transports.File({ 
      filename: path.join(__dirname, '../logs/combined.log') 
    })
  ]
});

// If we're not in production, log to the console as well
if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  logger.add(new winston.transports.Console({
    format: winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.colorize(),
      winston.format.simple()
    )
  }));
}

module.exports = logger;
```

**Step 11.3: Create Backup Script**
**File:** `scripts/backup.js`
```javascript
const { exec } = require('child_process');
const fs = require('fs');
const path = require('path');
const cron = require('node-cron');

const BACKUP_DIR = path.join(__dirname, '../backups');
const MONGODB_URI = process.env.MONGODB_URI;

// Create backup directory if it doesn't exist
if (!fs.existsSync(BACKUP_DIR)) {
  fs.mkdirSync(BACKUP_DIR, { recursive: true });
}

const createBackup = () => {
  const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-');
  const backupFile = path.join(BACKUP_DIR, `backup-${timestamp}.gz`);
  
  const command = `mongodump --uri="${MONGODB_URI}" --gzip --archive=${backupFile}`;
  
  exec(command, (error, stdout, stderr) => {
    if (error) {
      console.error(`Backup failed: ${error.message}`);
      return;
    }
    
    if (stderr) {
      console.error(`Backup stderr: ${stderr}`);
      return;
    }
    
    console.log(`Backup created: ${backupFile}`);
    
    // Clean up old backups (keep only last 7 days)
    const files = fs.readdirSync(BACKUP_DIR);
    const now = Date.now();
    const sevenDays = 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    
    files.forEach(file => {
      const filePath = path.join(BACKUP_DIR, file);
      const stats = fs.statSync(filePath);
      
      if (now - stats.mtimeMs > sevenDays) {
        fs.unlinkSync(filePath);
        console.log(`Deleted old backup: ${file}`);
      }
    });
  });
};

// Schedule daily backup at 2 AM
cron.schedule('0 2 * * *', createBackup);

module.exports = { createBackup };
```

## **ðŸ”§ TROUBLESHOOTING GUIDE**

### **Common Issues:**

1. **MongoDB Connection Failed:**
   ```bash
   # Check connection string
   echo $MONGODB_URI
   
   # Test connection
   mongosh "$MONGODB_URI" --eval "db.adminCommand('ping')"
   ```

2. **React Build Errors:**
   ```bash
   # Clear cache and reinstall
   cd client
   rm -rf node_modules package-lock.json
   npm cache clean --force
   npm install
   ```

3. **UAE Pass Integration Issues:**
   - Verify UAE Pass credentials
   - Check callback URL configuration
   - Test with staging environment first
   - Contact UAE Pass support if needed

4. **Deployment Issues:**
   ```bash
   # Check Vercel deployment logs
   vercel logs --follow
   
   # Redeploy
   vercel --prod
   ```
